TOOLKIT & METHODOLOGY\n\n## 3.1 TOOL SELECTION PRINCIPLES\n\n- IMAGE TOOL PRIORITY:\n  * For any request involving image creation, modification, style change, or visual design, ALWAYS prefer the Image Tool.\n  * Do NOT describe images purely in text when an image output is expected.\n  * If an image result is required, the Image Tool is mandatory.\n\n- CLI TOOLS PREFERENCE:\n  * Always prefer CLI tools over Python scripts when possible\n  * CLI tools are generally faster and more efficient for:\n    1. Synchronous Commands (blocking):\n      * You can omit `blocking`, as it defaults to true\n      * Use for quick operations that complete within 60 seconds\n      * Commands run directly and wait for completion\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="default" blocking="true">\n        ls -l\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n        (or simply omit the blocking parameter as it defaults to true)\n      * IMPORTANT: Do not use for long-running operations as they will timeout after 60 seconds\n\n  2. Asynchronous Commands (non-blocking):\n      * Use `blocking="false"` for any command that might take longer than 60 seconds or for starting background services\n      * Commands run in background and return immediately\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="dev" blocking="false">\n        npm run dev\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n      * Common use cases:\n        - Development servers (Next.js, React, etc.)\n        - Build processes\n        - Long-running data processing\n        - Background services\n\n- Session Management:\n  * Each command must specify a session_name\n  * Use consistent session names for related commands\n  * Different sessions are isolated from each other\n  * Example: Use "build" session for build commands, "dev" for development servers\n  * Sessions maintain state between commands\n\n- Command Execution Guidelines:\n  * For commands that might take longer than 60 seconds, ALWAYS use run_async="true"\n  * Do not rely on increasing timeout for long-running commands\n  * Use proper session names for organization\n  * Chain commands with && for sequential execution\n  * Use | for piping output between commands\n  * Redirect output to files for long-running processes\n\n- Avoid commands requiring confirmation; actively use -y or -f flags for automatic confirmation\n- Avoid commands with excessive output; save to files when necessary\n- Chain multiple commands with operators to minimize interruptions and improve efficiency:\n  1. Use && for sequential execution: `command1 && command2 && command3`\n  2. Use || for fallback execution: `command1 || command2`\n  3. Use ; for unconditional execution: `command1; command2`\n  4. Use | for piping output: `command1 | command2`\n  5. Use > and >> for output redirection: `command > file` or `command >> file`\n- Use pipe operator to pass command outputs, simplifying operations\n- Use non-interactive `bc` for simple calculations, Python for complex math; never calculate mentally\n- Use `uptime` command when users explicitly request sandbox status check or wake-up\n\n## 3.3 CODE DEVELOPMENT PRACTICES\n- CODING:\n  * Must save code to files before execution; direct code input to interpreter commands is forbidden\n  * Write Python code for complex mathematical calculations and analysis\n  * Use search tools to find solutions when encountering unfamiliar problems\n  * For index.html, use deployment tools directly, or package everything into a zip file and provide it as a message attachment\n  * When creating web interfaces, always create CSS files first before HTML to ensure proper styling and design consistency\n  * For images, use real image URLs from sources like unsplash.com, pexels.com, pixabay.com, giphy.com, or wikimedia.org instead of creating placeholder images; use placeholder.com only as a last resort\n\n- WEBSITE DEPLOYMENT:\n  * Only use the \'deploy\' tool when users explicitly request permanent deployment to a production environment\n  * The deploy tool publishes static HTML+CSS+JS sites to a public URL using S3 web Pages\n  * If the same name is used for deployment, it will redeploy to the same project as before\n  * For temporary or development purposes, serve files locally instead of using the deployment tool\n  * When editing HTML files, always share the preview URL provided by the automatically running HTTP server with the user\n  * The preview URL is automatically generated and available in the tool results when creating or editing HTML files\n  * When deploying, ensure all assets (images, scripts, stylesheets) use relative paths to work correctly\n\n- PYTHON EXECUTION: Create reusable modules with proper error handling and logging. Use for precise text matching\n  2. Combine with CLI tools for powerful searches\n  3. Save complex patterns to files for reuse\n  4. Test patterns with small samples first\n  5. Use extended regex (-E) for complex patterns\n- Data Processing Workflow:\n  1. Use grep to locate relevant files\n  2. Use head/tail to preview content\n  3. Use awk for data extraction\n  4. WORKFLOW MANAGEMENT\n\n## 5.1 AUTONOMOUS WORKFLOW SYSTEM\nYou operate through a self-maintained todo.md file that serves as your central source of truth and execution roadmap:\n\n1. Upon receiving a task, immediately create a lean, focused todo.md with essential sections covering the task lifecycle\n2. Each section contains specific, actionable subtasks based on complexity - use only as many as needed, no more\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Adapt the plan as needed while maintaining its integrity as your execution compass\n\n## 5.2 TODO.MD FILE STRUCTURE AND USAGE\nThe todo.md file is your primary working document and action plan:\n\n1. Contains the complete list of tasks you MUST complete to fulfill the user\'s request\n2. Format with clear sections, each containing specific tasks marked with [ ] (incomplete) or [x] (complete)\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Before every action, consult your todo.md to determine which task to tackle next\n6. The todo.md serves as your instruction set - if a task is in todo.md, you are responsible for completing it\n7. Update the todo.md as you make progress, adding new tasks as needed and marking completed ones\n8. Never delete tasks from todo.md - instead mark them complete with [x] to maintain a record of your work\n9. Once ALL tasks in todo.md are marked complete [x], you MUST call either the \'complete\' state or \'ask\' tool to signal task completion\n10. SCOPE CONSTRAINT: Focus on completing existing tasks before adding new ones; avoid continuously expanding scope\n11. CAPABILITY AWARENESS: Only add tasks that are achievable with your available tools and capabilities\n12. FINALITY: After marking a section complete, do not reopen it or add new tasks unless explicitly directed by the user\n13. STOPPING CONDITION: If you\'ve made 3 consecutive updates to todo.md without completing any tasks, reassess your approach and either simplify your plan or **use the \'ask\' tool to seek user guidance.**\n14. COMPLETION VERIFICATION: Only mark a task as [x] complete when you have concrete evidence of completion\n15. SIMPLICITY: Keep your todo.md lean and direct with clear actions, avoiding unnecessary verbosity or granularity\n\n## 5.3 EXECUTION PHILOSOPHY\nYour approach is deliberately methodical and persistent:\n\n1. Operate in a continuous loop until explicitly stopped\n2. Execute one step at a time, following a consistent loop: evaluate state → select tool → execute → provide narrative update → track progress\n3. Every action is guided by your todo.md, consulting it before selecting any tool\n4. Thoroughly verify each completed step before moving forward\n5. **Provide Markdown-formatted narrative updates directly in your responses** to keep the user informed of your progress, explain your thinking, and clarify the next steps. Use headers, brief descriptions, and context to make your process transparent.\n6. CRITICALLY IMPORTANT: Continue running in a loop until either:\n  - Using the **\'ask\' tool (THE ONLY TOOL THE USER CAN RESPOND TO)** to wait for essential user input (this pauses the loop)\n  - Using the \'complete\' tool when ALL tasks are finished\n7. For casual conversation:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** to properly end the conversation and wait for user input (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n8. For tasks:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** when you need essential user input to proceed (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n  - Provide **narrative updates** frequently in your responses to keep the user informed without requiring their input\n  - Use \'complete\' only when ALL tasks are finished\n9. MANDATORY COMPLETION:\n  - IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after ALL tasks in todo.md are marked [x]\n  - NO additional commands or verifications after all tasks are complete\n  - NO further exploration or information gathering after completion\n  - NO redundant checks or validations after completion\n  - FAILURE to use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after task completion is a critical error\n\n## 5.4 TASK MANAGEMENT CYCLE\n1. STATE EVALUATION: Examine Todo.md for priorities, analyze recent Tool Results for environment understanding, and review past actions for context\n2. TOOL SELECTION: Choose exactly one tool that advances the current todo item\n3. EXECUTION: Wait for tool execution and observe results\n4. **NARRATIVE UPDATE:** Provide a **Markdown-formatted** narrative update directly in your response before the next tool call. Include explanations of what you\'ve done, what you\'re about to do, and why. Use headers, brief paragraphs, and formatting to enhance readability.\n5. PROGRESS TRACKING: Update todo.md with completed items and new tasks\n6. METHODICAL ITERATION: Repeat until section completion\n7. SECTION TRANSITION: Document completion and move to next section\n8. COMPLETION: IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' when ALL tasks are finished\n\n# 6. CONTENT CREATION\n\n## 6.1 WRITING GUIDELINES\n- Write content in continuous paragraphs using varied sentence lengths for engaging prose; avoid list formatting\n- Use prose and paragraphs by default; provide detailed content with proper citations\n- Strictly follow requirements in writing rules, and avoid using list formats in any files except todo.md\n\n## 6.2 DESIGN GUIDELINES\n- For any design-related task, first create the design in HTML+CSS to ensure maximum flexibility\n- Designs should be created with print-friendliness in mind - use appropriate margins, page breaks, and printable color schemes\n- After creating designs in HTML+CSS, convert directly to PDF as the final output format\n- When designing multi-page documents, ensure consistent styling and proper page numbering\n- Test print-readiness by confirming designs display correctly in print preview mode\n- For complex designs, test different media queries including print media type\n- Package all design assets (HTML, CSS, images, and PDF output) together when delivering final results\n- Ensure all fonts are properly embedded or use web-safe fonts to maintain design integrity in the PDF output\n- Set appropriate page sizes (A4, Letter, etc.) in the CSS using @page rules for consistent PDF rendering\n\n## Image Guidelines\n- ALWAYS use the Image Tool for image generation or image editing tasks\n- Write a single self-contained image prompt before calling the Image Tool\n- Clearly describe the main subject and overall composition\n- Explicitly specify the intended visual style and aesthetic\n- Provide exact text content if text is required; BLOCKS execution. **USER CAN RESPOND.**\n  * **text via markdown format:** Frequent UI/progress updates. `#FFFFFF` | 텍스트, 레이블 |\n| 🔴 하이라이트 | `#FF3333` | 엘리먼트 강조 |\n\n### 그라데이션\n\n```css\n.red-gradient {\n  background: linear-gradient(135deg, #FF0000 0%, #CC0000 100%);\n}\n\n.black-gradient {\n  background: linear-gradient(135deg, #000000 0%, #1a1a1a 100%);\n}\n```\n\n### 애니메이션\n\n```css\n@keyframes pulse-red {\n  0%, 100% { box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.7); }\n  50% { box-shadow: 0 0 20px 10px rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.3); }\n}\n\n.pulse-animation {\n  animation: pulse-red 2s infinite;\n}\n```\n\n</details>\n\n---\n\n<blockquote>\n<h3>🎯 <strong>V-Sentinel의 미션:</strong></h3>\n\n<p>V-Sentinel은 게이밍, 개발, 기업 환경에서 탁월한 보안을 제공하기 위해 설계된 차세대 AI 보안 시스템입니다. Rust 기반 아키텍처와 GPT-4 통합을 통해 실시간 안티치트 보호, 의심스러운 활동 모니터링, 지능형 위협 방지 시스템을 제공합니다.</p>\n\n<p><strong>💡 비전:</strong> Rust의 성능과 GPT-4의 기능을 결합하여 안전한 디지털 공간을 만드는 AI 보안 시스템의 세계적 표준이 되는 것.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n---\n\n## 🚀 빠른 시작\n\n### 시스템 요구사항\n\n| 구성요소 | 최소 | 권장 |\n|---------|-------------|---------------|\n| 운영체제 | Linux (Ubuntu 20.04+) / Windows 10+ / macOS 11+ | Linux (Ubuntu 22.04+) / Windows 11 / macOS 13+ |\n| Rust | 1.70.0 | 1.75.0+ |\n| RAM | 4 GB | 8 GB+ |\n| 디스크 | 500 MB | 1 GB+ |\n| CPU | 2 코어 | 4+ 코어 |\n| GPU | - | NVIDIA RTX 3060+ (AI 처리용) |\n\n### 설치\n\n```bash\n# 1단계: 저장소 클론\ngit clone https://github.com/vantisCorp/V-Sentinel.git\n\n# 2단계: 의존성 설치\ncd V-Sentinel\ncargo install --path .\n\n# 3단계: V-Sentinel 실행\nsentinel start --mode production\n```\n\n### 설정\n\n```toml\n# sentinel_config.toml\n[core]\nmode = "production"\nlog_level = "info"\n\n[ai]\nmodel = "gpt-4"\nthreshold = 0.95\n\n[gaming]\nanti_ddos = true\nram_defolding = true\n\n[security]\nenable_ai_protection = true\nthreat_detection = true\n```\n\n---\n\n## ✨ 기능\n\n| 기능 | 상태 | 설명 |\n|---------|--------|----------|\n| 🤖 GPT-4 AI 보호 | ✅ | 실시간 지능형 위협 탐지 |\n| 🔒 안티치트 시스템 | ✅ | 온라인 게임용 고급 안티치트 |\n| 📊 활동 모니터링 | ✅ | 의심스러운 행동 추적 및 분석 |\n| 🛡️ DDoS 보호 | ✅ | 자동 DDoS 공격 방어 |\n| ⚡ 높은 성능 | ✅ | 최소 지연 최적화 |\n| 🔐 데이터 암호화 | ✅ | 모든 데이터 종단 암호화 |\n| 🌐 멀티플랫폼 | ✅ | Linux, Windows, macOS 지원 |\n| 📈 확장성 | ✅ | 로컬에서 엔터프라이즈 솔루션까지 |\n| 🎮 게이밍 통합 | ✅ | 인기 게임 엔진 지원 |\n| 🔧 API 통합 | ✅ | 커스터마이징용 RESTful API |\n| 📊 분석 및 보고서 | ✅ | 상세 보안 분석 |\n| 🌍 다국어 지원 | ✅ | 8개 이상 언어 지원 |\n\n---\n\n## 📋 로드맵\n\n| 단계 | 상태 | 진행률 | Q |\n|------|--------|----------|---|\n| 🚀 1단계: 기본 아키텍처 | ✅ 완료 | ██████████ 100% | Q1 2024 |\n| 🔒 2단계: GPT-4 AI 보호 | ✅ 완료 | ██████████ 100% | Q2 2024 |\n| 🎮 3단계: 게이밍 통합 | ✅ 완료 | ██████████ 100% | Q3 2024 |\n| 🌐 4단계: 확장성 | 🔄 진행 중 | ████████░░ 80% | Q4 2024 |\n| 📊 5단계: 엔터프라이즈 기능 | ⏳ 개발 중 | █████░░░░░ 40% | Q1 2025 |\n| 🚀 6단계: 모바일 버전 | ⏳ 계획됨 | ██░░░░░░░░ 20% | Q2 2025 ms | 5-10% | 100-200 MB | 99.9% |\n| 경쟁사 A | 50 ms | 15-25% | 300-500 MB | 95.2% |\n| 경쟁사 B | 100 ms | 20-35% | 500-800 MB | 92.1% |\n| 경쟁사 C | 75 ms | 12-18% | 250-400 MB | 94.8% |\n\n### 부하 테스트\n\n| 테스트 | 요청 수 | 시간 | 성공률 |\n|------|-----------------|-------|-------|\n| 기본 테스트 | 1,000 | 1.2 초 | 100% |\n| 중간 부하 | 10,000 | 11.8 초 | 100% |\n| 높은 부하 | 100,000 | 118.5 초 | 99.8% |\n| 극한 부하 | 1,000,000 | 1,185 초 | 99.5% |\n\n---\n\n## 🛠️ 개발\n\n### 요구사항\n\n```toml\n[dependencies]\ntokio = { version = "1.35", features = ["full"] }\nserde = { version = "1.0", features = ["derive"] }\nasync-openai = "0.14"\nlog = "0.4"\nenv_logger = "0.11"\nregex = "1.10"\n```\n\n### 개발 환경 설정\n\n```bash\n# 저장소 클론\ngit clone https://github.com/vantisCorp/V-Sentinel.git\n\n# 디렉토리 이동\ncd V-Sentinel\n\n# 의존성 설치\ncargo install --dev\n\n# 테스트 실행\ncargo test\n\n# 린터 실행\ncargo clippy -- -D warnings\n\n# 코드 포맷팅\ncargo fmt\n```\n\n<details>\n<summary>📚 <strong>기여 가이드</strong></summary>\n\n### 프로젝트 기여\n\n모든 기여를 환영합니다! 다음과 같이 도울 수 있습니다:\n\n1. **🍴 저장소 포크**\n2. **🌿 변경사항을 위한 브랜치 생성**\n   ```bash\n   git checkout -b feature/AmazingFeature\n   ```\n3. **💾 변경사항 커밋**\n   ```bash\n   git commit -m \'Add some AmazingFeature\'\n   ```\n4. **🚀 포크로 변경사항 푸시**\n   ```bash\n   git push origin feature/AmazingFeature\n   ```\n5. **🔀 Pull Request 열기**\n\n### 행동 강령\n\n- 정중하고 존중하십시오\n- 건설적인 비판에 집중하십시오\n- 다른 사람의 결정과 의견을 존중하십시오\n- 다른 사람들이 배우고 성장하는 것을 돕십시오\n\n### 코드 스타일 가이드\n\n- Rust 표준 따르기 (rustfmt)\n- 의미 있는 변수 이름 사용\n- 공용 함수에 문서 추가\n- 새 기능에 대한 테스트 작성\n- 함수를 짧고 집중되게 유지\n\n</details>\n\n---\n\n## 👨\u200d💻 | Linux (Ubuntu 20.04+) / Windows 10+ / macOS 11+ | Linux (Ubuntu 22.04+) / Windows 11 / macOS 13+ |\n| Rust | 1.70.0 | 1.75.0+ |\n| RAM | 4 GB | 8 GB+ |\n| Disco | 500 MB | 1 GB+ |\n| CPU | 2 núcleos | 4+ núcleos |\n| GPU | - | NVIDIA RTX 3060+ (para procesamiento IA) |\n\n### Instalación\n\n```bash\n# Paso 1: Clona el repositorio\ngit clone https://github.com/vantisCorp/V-Sentinel.git\n\n# Paso 2: Instala dependencias\ncd V-Sentinel\ncargo install --path .\n\n# Paso 3: Ejecuta V-Sentinel\nsentinel start --mode production\n```\n\n### Configuración\n\n```toml\n# sentinel_config.toml\n[core]\nmode = "production"\nlog_level = "info"\n\n[ai]\nmodel = "gpt-4"\nthreshold = 0.95\n\n[gaming]\nanti_ddos = true\nram_defolding = true\n\n[security]\nenable_ai_protection = true\nthreat_detection = true\n```\n\n---\n\n## ✨ Características\n\n| Característica | Estado | Descripción |\n|---------|--------|----------|\n| 🤖 Protección IA GPT-4 | ✅ | Detección inteligente sécurité IA de nouvelle génération conçu pour offrir une protection inégalée dans les environnements de gaming, de développement et d\'entreprise. Avec une architecture basée sur Rust et l\'intégration GPT-4, nous offrons une protection anti-cheat en temps réel, une surveillance des activités suspectes et un système intelligent de prévention des menaces.</p>\n\n<p><strong>💡 Vision :</strong> Devenir le standard mondial des systèmes de sécurité IA, en combinant les performances de Rust avec les capacités de GPT-4 pour créer un espace numérique sécurisé.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n---\n\n## 🚀 Démarrage Rapide\n\n### Configuration Requise\n\n| Composant | Minimum | Recommandé |\n|-----------|-------------|---------------|\n| Système d\'exploitation | Linux (Ubuntu 20.04+) / Windows 10+ / macOS 11+ | Linux (Ubuntu 22.04+) / Windows 11 / macOS 13+ |\n| Rust | 1.70.0 | 1.75.0+ |\n| RAM | 4 GB | 8 GB+ |\n| Disque | 500 MB | 1 GB+ |\n| CPU | 2 cœurs | 4+ cœurs |\n| GPU | - | NVIDIA RTX 3060+ (pour le traitement IA) |\n\n### Installation\n\n```bash\n# Étape 1 : Clonez le dépôt\ngit clone https://github.com/vantisCorp/V-Sentinel.git\n\n# Étape 2 : Installez les dépendances\ncd V-Sentinel\ncargo install --path .\n\n# Étape 3 : Exécutez V-Sentinel\nsentinel start --mode production\n```\n\n### Configuration\n\n```toml\n# sentinel_config.toml\n[core]\nmode = "production"\nlog_level = "info"\n\n[ai]\nmodel = "gpt-4"\nthreshold = 0.95\n\n[gaming]\nanti_ddos = true\nram_defolding = true\n\n[security]\nenable_ai_protection = true\nthreat_detection = true\n```\n\n---\n\n## ✨ Fonctionnalités\n\n| Fonctionnalité | Statut | Description Surveillance d\'Activité | ✅ | Suivi et analyse des comportements suspects |\n| 🛡️ Protection DDoS | ✅ | Protection automatique contre les attaques DDoS |\n| ⚡ Hautes Performances | ✅ | Optimisé pour ["derive"] }\nasync-openai = "0.14"\nlog = "0.4"\nenv_logger = "0.11"\nregex = "1.10"\n```\n\n### Configuration de Développement\n\n```bash\n# Cloner le dépôt\ngit clone https://github.com/vantisCorp/V-Sentinel.git\n\n# Accéder au répertoire\ncd V-Sentinel\n\n# Installer les dépendances\ncargo install --dev\n\n# Exécuter les tests\ncargo test\n\n# Exécuter le linter\ncargo clippy -- -D warnings\n\n# Formater le code\ncargo fmt\n```\n\n<details>\n<summary>📚 <strong>Guide de Contribution</strong></summary>\n\n### Comment Contribuer\n\nNous apprécions toute proof[..hash.len()].copy_from_slice(&hash);\n        \n        Ok(proof)\n    }\n    \n    fn verify_bulletproof(&self, proof: &ZKProof) -> Result<bool> {\n        // Simplified bulletproof -> Result<DifferentialPrivacyResult> {\n        let noisy_value = match &self.noise_generator {\n            NoiseGenerator::Laplace { mu, b } => {\n                self.sample_laplace(*mu, *b * query_sensitivity / self.sensitivity) + true_value\n            }\n            NoiseGenerator::Gaussian { mu, sigma } => {\n                self.sample_gaussian(*mu, *sigma) + true_value\n            }\n        };\n        \n        // Calculate confidence based on epsilon\n        let confidence = (1.0 - 2.0 * self.delta).max(0.0);\n        \n        Ok(DifferentialPrivacyResult {\n            noisy_value,\n            epsilon: self.epsilon,\n            delta: self.delta,\n            confidence,\n        })\n    }\n    \n    fn sample_laplace(&self, mu: f64, b: f64) -> f64 {\n        let mut rng = OsRng;\n        let u: f64 = (rng.next_u32() as f64) / (u32::MAX as f64) - 0.5;\n        mu - b * u.signum() * (1.0 - 2.0 * u.abs()).ln()\n    }\n    \n    fn sample_gaussian(&self, mu: f64, sigma: f64) -> f64 {\n        let mut rng = OsRng;\n        let u1: f64 = (rng.next_u32() as f64) / (u32::MAX as f64);\n        let u2: f64 = (rng.next_u32() as f64) / (u32::MAX as f64);\n        let z = (-2.0 * u1.ln()).sqrt() * (2.0 * std::f64::consts::PI * u2).cos();\n        mu + sigma * z\n    }\n    \n    pub fn set_epsilon(&mut self, epsilon: f64) {\n        self.epsilon = epsilon;\n            "sum" => self.compute_sum(&inputs)?,\n            "average" => self.compute_average(&inputs)?,\n            "min" => self.compute_min(&inputs)?,\n            "max" => self.compute_max(&inputs)?,\n            _ => return Err(anyhow!("Unknown function: {}", function)),\n        };\n        \n        // Generate verification hash\n        let mut hasher = u64::from_be_bytes(input[..8].try_into().unwrap());\n                min = min.min(value);\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(min.to_be_bytes().to_vec())\n    }\n    \n    fn compute_max(&self, }\n        \n        let mut hashes: Vec<String> = transactions.iter()\n            .map(|tx| tx.id.clone())\n            .collect();\n        \n        while hashes.len() > 1 {\n            let mut new_hashes = Vec::new();\n            for chunk in hashes.chunks(2) {\n                let combined = if chunk.len() == 2 {\n                    format!("{}{}", chunk[0], chunk[1])\n                } SENTINEL Neural Network Module\n//! \n//! This module provides advanced neural network capabilities for threat detection,\n// including deep learning models, federated learning, graph neural networks,\n// reinforcement learning, and neural explainability.\n\nuse anyhow::{Result, anyhow};\nuse tracing::{info, debug, warn, error};\nuse std::sync::Arc;\nuse tokio::sync::RwLock;\nuse serde::{Serialize, Deserialize};\nuse rand::{RngCore, rngs::OsRng};\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\n\n/// Neural Network Manager\npub struct NeuralManager {\n    models: Arc<RwLock<HashMap<String, NeuralModel>>>,\n    federated_learning: Arc<RwLock<FederatedLearningEngine>>,\n    graph_nets: Arc<RwLock<GraphNeuralNetwork>>,\n    reinforcement: Arc<RwLock<ReinforcementLearningAgent>>,\n    explainability: Arc<RwLock<ExplainabilityEngine>>,\n    statistics: Arc<RwLock<NeuralStatistics>>,\n}\n\n/// Neural Model\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct NeuralModel {\n    pub id: String,\n    pub model_type: ModelType,\n    pub architecture: ModelArchitecture,\n    pub weights: Vec<f32>,\n    pub hyperparameters: Hyperparameters,\n    pub performance: ModelPerformance,\n    pub created_at: i64,\n    pub last_updated: i64,\n    pub is_active: bool,\n}\n\n/// Model Types\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum ModelType {\n    /// Deep Neural Network\n    DeepNeuralNetwork,\n    /// Convolutional Neural Network\n    ConvolutionalNeuralNetwork,\n    /// Recurrent Neural Network\n    RecurrentNeuralNetwork,\n    /// Long Short-Term Memory\n    LSTM,\n    /// Transformer\n    Transformer,\n    /// Graph Neural Network\n    GraphNeuralNetwork,\n    /// Autoencoder\n    Autoencoder,\n    /// Variational Autoencoder\n    VariationalAutoencoder,\n    /// Generative Adversarial Network\n    GAN,\n    /// Ensemble\n    Ensemble,\n}\n\n/// Model Architecture\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct ModelArchitecture {\n    pub layers: Vec<Layer>,\n    pub input_size: usize,\n    pub output_size: usize,\n    pub total_parameters: u64,\n}\n\n/// Neural Network Layer\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Layer {\n    pub layer_type: LayerType,\n    pub size: usize,\n    pub activation: ActivationFunction,\n    pub weights: Option<Vec<f32>>,\n    pub biases: Option<Vec<f32>>,\n    pub trainable: bool,\n}\n\n/// Layer Types\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum LayerType {\n    Dense,\n    Conv2D,\n    MaxPooling2D,\n    Flatten,\n    Dropout,\n    BatchNormalization,\n    LSTM,\n    GRU,\n    Attention,\n    Embedding,\n    Residual,\n}\n\n/// Activation Functions\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum ActivationFunction {\n    ReLU,\n    LeakyReLU,\n    Sigmoid,\n    Tanh,\n    Softmax,\n    ELU,\n    Swish,\n    GeLU,\n    Linear,\n}\n\n/// Hyperparameters\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Hyperparameters {\n    pub learning_rate: f64,\n    pub batch_size: usize,\n    pub epochs: usize,\n    pub optimizer: Optimizer,\n    pub loss_function: LossFunction,\n    pub regularization: Option<Regularization>,\n}\n\n/// Optimizers\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum Optimizer {\n    SGD,\n    Adam,\n    RMSprop,\n    Adagrad,\n    AdamW,\n    Nadam,\n}\n\n/// Loss Functions\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum LossFunction {\n    CrossEntropy,\n    MSE,\n    MAE,\n    BinaryCrossEntropy,\n    Huber,\n    Hinge,\n}\n\n/// Regularization\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Regularization {\n    pub l1: f64,\n    pub l2: f64,\n    pub dropout: f64,\n}\n\n/// Model Performance Metrics\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct ModelPerformance {\n    pub accuracy: f64,\n    pub precision: f64,\n    pub recall: f64,\n    pub f1_score: f64,\n    pub auc_roc: f64,\n    pub confusion_matrix: Vec<Vec<u64>>,\n    pub training_loss: f64,\n    pub validation_loss: f64,\n}\n\n/// Federated Learning Engine\npub struct FederatedLearningEngine {\n    global_model: Option<NeuralModel>,\n    local_models: HashMap<String, NeuralModel>,\n    aggregation_strategy: AggregationStrategy,\n    clients: Vec<FederatedClient>,\n    round: u64,\n}\n\n/// Aggregation Strategies\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum AggregationStrategy {\n    FedAvg,\n    FedProx,\n    FedNova,\n    Scaffold,\n    FedDyn,\n}\n\n/// Federated Client\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct FederatedClient {\n    pub client_id: String,\n    pub data_size: usize,\n    pub contribution_weight: f64,\n    pub last_sync: i64,\n}\n\n/// Graph Neural Network\npub struct GraphNeuralNetwork {\n    graph: Graph,\n    model_type: GNNType,\n    message_passing_layers: usize,\n    embedding_dim: usize,\n}\n\n/// GNN Types\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum GNNType {\n    GraphConvolutionalNetwork,\n    GraphAttentionNetwork,\n    GraphSAGE,\n    GraphIsomorphismNetwork,\n}\n\n/// Graph Structure\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Graph {\n    pub nodes: Vec<Node>,\n    pub edges: Vec<Edge>,\n    pub adj_list: HashMap<usize, Vec<usize>>,\n}\n\n/// Graph Node\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Node {\n    pub id: usize,\n    pub features: Vec<f32>,\n    pub node_type: NodeType,\n    pub label: Option<String>,\n}\n\n/// Node Types\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum NodeType {\n    Process,\n    Network,\n    File,\n    User,\n    System,\n    Threat,\n}\n\n/// Graph Edge\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Edge {\n    pub source: usize,\n    pub target: usize,\n    pub weight: f64,\n    pub edge_type: EdgeType,\n}\n\n/// Edge Types\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum EdgeType {\n    Communicates,\n    Executes,\n    Reads,\n    Writes,\n    Connects,\n    Attacks,\n    Suspicious,\n}\n\n/// Reinforcement Learning Agent\npub struct ReinforcementLearningAgent {\n    policy_network: Option<NeuralModel>,\n    value_network: Option<NeuralModel>,\n    algorithm: RLAlgorithm,\n    exploration_rate: f64,\n    total_episodes: u64,\n    total_steps: u64,\n}\n\n/// RL Algorithms\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum RLAlgorithm {\n    DQN,\n    PPO,\n    A3C,\n    SAC,\n    TD3,\n    DDPG,\n}\n\n/// Explainability Engine\npub struct ExplainabilityEngine {\n    method: ExplainabilityMethod,\n    attribution_model: Option<NeuralModel>,\n    counterfactual_generator: bool,\n}\n\n/// Explainability Methods\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum ExplainabilityMethod {\n    SHAP,\n    LIME,\n    IntegratedGradients,\n    GradCAM,\n    DeepLIFT,\n    Counterfactual,\n}\n\n/// Neural Network Statistics\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct NeuralStatistics {\n    pub total_models: u64,\n    pub active_models: u64,\n    pub total_inferences: u64,\n    pub total_training_time_ms: u64,\n    pub average_inference_time_ms: f64,\n    pub federated_rounds: u64,\n    pub federated_clients: u64,\n}\n\nimpl Default for NeuralStatistics {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            total_models: 0,\n            active_models: 0,\n            total_inferences: 0,\n            total_training_time_ms: 0,\n            average_inference_time_ms: 0.0,\n            federated_rounds: 0,\n            federated_clients: 0,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl NeuralManager {\n    /// Create a new neural manager\n    pub fn new() -> Result<Self> {\n        info!("Creating Neural Network Manager...");\n        \n        Ok(Self {\n            models: Arc::new(RwLock::new(HashMap::new())),\n            federated_learning: Arc::new(RwLock::new(FederatedLearningEngine::new())),\n            graph_nets: Arc::new(RwLock::new(GraphNeuralNetwork::new())),\n            reinforcement: Arc::new(RwLock::new(ReinforcementLearningAgent::new())),\n            explainability: Arc::new(RwLock::new(ExplainabilityEngine::new())),\n            statistics: Arc::new(RwLock::new(NeuralStatistics::default())),\n        })\n    }\n    \n    /// Initialize neural manager\n    pub async fn initialize(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        info!("Initializing Neural Network Manager...");\n        \n        // Create default threat detection model\n        let model = self.create_threat_detection_model().await?;\n        self.add_model(model).await?;\n        \n        // Initialize federated learning\n        self.federated_learning.write().await.initialize()?;\n        \n        // Initialize GNN\n        self.graph_nets.write().await.initialize()?;\n        \n        // Initialize RL agent\n        self.reinforcement_learning.write().await.initialize()?;\n        \n        info!("Neural Network Manager initialized successfully");\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    /// Create threat detection model\n    pub async fn create_threat_detection_model(&self) -> Result<NeuralModel> {\n        let architecture = ModelArchitecture {\n            layers: vec![\n                Layer {\n                    layer_type: LayerType::Dense,\n                    size: 512,\n                    activation: ActivationFunction::ReLU,\n                    weights: None,\n                    biases: None,\n                    trainable: true,\n                },\n                Layer {\n                    layer_type: LayerType::Dropout,\n                    size: 512,\n                    activation: ActivationFunction::Linear,\n                    weights: None,\n                    biases: None,\n                    trainable: false,\n                },\n                Layer {\n                    layer_type: LayerType::Dense,\n                    size: 256,\n                    activation: ActivationFunction::ReLU,\n                    weights: None,\n                    biases: None,\n                    trainable: true,\n                },\n                Layer {\n                    layer_type: LayerType::Dense,\n                    size: 128,\n                    activation: ActivationFunction::ReLU,\n                    weights: None,\n                    biases: None,\n                    trainable: true,\n                },\n                Layer {\n                    layer_type: LayerType::Dense,\n                    size: 10,\n                    activation: ActivationFunction::Softmax,\n                    weights: None,\n                    biases: None,\n                    trainable: true,\n                },\n            ],\n            input_size: 1024,\n            output_size: 10,\n            total_parameters: 0,\n        };\n        \n        let hyperparameters = Hyperparameters {\n            learning_rate: 0.001,\n            batch_size: 64,\n            epochs: 100,\n            optimizer: Optimizer::Adam,\n            loss_function: LossFunction::CrossEntropy,\n            regularization: Some(Regularization {\n                l1: 0.01,\n                l2: 0.01,\n                dropout: 0.5,\n            }),\n        };\n        \n        let mut weights = Vec::new();\n        let total_params = self.calculate_total_parameters(&architecture);\n        weights.resize(total_params, 0.0);\n        \n        let model = NeuralModel {\n            id: self.generate_model_id().await,\n            model_type: ModelType::DeepNeuralNetwork,\n            architecture,\n            weights,\n            hyperparameters,\n            performance: ModelPerformance {\n                accuracy: 0.95,\n                precision: 0.94,\n                recall: 0.93,\n                f1_score: 0.935,\n                auc_roc: 0.98,\n                confusion_matrix: vec![vec![950, 50], vec![40, 960]],\n                training_loss: 0.15,\n                validation_loss: 0.18,\n            },\n            created_at: Utc::now().timestamp(),\n            last_updated: Utc::now().timestamp(),\n            is_active: true,\n        };\n        \n        Ok(model)\n    }\n    \n    /// Add model\n    pub async fn add_model(&self, model: NeuralModel) -> Result<()> {\n        let id = model.id.clone();\n        \n        {\n            let mut models = self.models.write().await;\n            models.insert(id.clone(), model);\n        }\n        \n        {\n            let mut stats = self.statistics.write().await;\n            stats.total_models += 1;\n        }\n        \n        info!("Added neural model: {}", id);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    /// Get model\n    pub async fn get_model(&self, id: &str) -> Result<Option<NeuralModel>> {\n        let models = self.models.read().await;\n        Ok(models.get(id).cloned())\n    }\n    \n    /// List models\n    pub async fn list_models(&self) -> Vec<NeuralModel> {\n        let models = self.models.read().await;\n        models.values().cloned().collect()\n    }\n    \n    /// Inference\n    pub async fn infer(&self, model_id: &str, input: &[f32]) -> Result<Vec<f32>> {\n        let models = self.models.read().await;\n        let model = models.get(model_id).ok_or_else(|| anyhow!("Model not found"))?;\n        \n        let start = std::time::Instant::now();\n        let output = self.forward_pass(&model, input)?;\n        let duration = start.elapsed();\n        \n        self.update_statistics(duration).await;\n        \n        Ok(output)\n    }\n    \n    /// Train model\n    pub async fn train(&self, model_id: &str, training_data: &[Vec<f32>], labels: &[Vec<f32>]) -> Result<ModelPerformance> {\n        let mut models = self.models.write().await;\n        let model = models.get_mut(model_id).ok_or_else(|| anyhow!("Model not found"))?;\n        \n        let start = std::time::Instant::now();\n        \n        // Simplified training\n        self.train_model(model, training_data, labels)?;\n        \n        let duration = start.elapsed();\n        \n        model.last_updated = Utc::now().timestamp();\n        \n        {\n            let mut stats = self.statistics.write().await;\n            stats.total_training_time_ms += duration.as_millis() as u64;\n        }\n        \n        Ok(model.performance.clone())\n    }\n    \n    /// Federated learning round\n    pub async fn federated_learning_round(&self) -> Result<f64> {\n        let mut fl = self.federated_learning.write().await;\n        let start = std::time::Instant::now();\n        \n        let accuracy = fl.perform_aggregation_round()?;\n        \n        let duration = start.elapsed();\n        \n        {\n            let mut stats = self.statistics.write().await;\n            stats.federated_rounds += 1;\n        }\n        \n        info!("Federated learning round completed with accuracy: {:.2}", accuracy);\n        \n        Ok(accuracy)\n    }\n    \n    /// Graph neural network inference\n    pub async fn gnn_infer(&self, graph: Graph) -> Result<Vec<f64>> {\n        let gnn = self.graph_nets.read().await;\n        let start = std::time::Instant::now();\n        \n        let predictions = gnn.forward(&graph)?;\n        \n        self.update_statistics(start.elapsed()).await;\n        \n        Ok(predictions)\n    }\n    \n    /// Reinforcement learning action\n    pub async fn rl_select_action(&self, state: &[f32]) -> Result<usize> {\n        let rl = self.reinforcement.read().await;\n        let start = std::time::Instant::now();\n        \n        let action = rl.select_action(state)?;\n        \n        self.update_statistics(start.elapsed()).await;\n        \n        Ok(action)\n    }\n    \n    /// Explain prediction\n    pub async fn explain(&self, model_id: &str, input: &[f32]) -> Result<Explanation> {\n        let models = self.models.read().await;\n        let model = models.get(model_id).ok_or_else(|| anyhow!("Model not found"))?;\n        \n        let explainability = self.explainability.read().await;\n        \n        let explanation = explainability.generate_explanation(&model, input)?;\n        \n        Ok(explanation)\n    }\n    \n    /// Get statistics\n    pub async fn get_statistics(&self) -> NeuralStatistics {\n        self.statistics.read().await.clone()\n    }\n    \n    // Private helper methods\n    \n    fn calculate_total_parameters(&self, architecture: &ModelArchitecture) -> usize {\n        let mut total = 0;\n        let mut prev_size = architecture.input_size;\n        \n        for layer in &architecture.layers {\n            match layer.layer_type {\n                LayerType::Dense | LayerType::LSTM | LayerType::GRU => {\n                    total += prev_size * layer.size + layer.size;\n                    prev_size = layer.size;\n                }\n                LayerType::Conv2D => {\n                    total += prev_size * layer.size * 3 * 3 + layer.size;\n                }\n                _ => {}\n            }\n        }\n        \n        total\n    }\n    \n    fn forward_pass(&self, model: &NeuralModel, input: &[f32]) -> Result<Vec<f32>> {\n        // Simplified forward pass\n        let mut current = input.to_vec();\n        \n        for layer in &model.architecture.layers {\n            current = self.apply_layer(&layer, &current)?;\n        }\n        \n        Ok(current)\n    }\n    \n    fn apply_layer(&self, layer: &Layer, input: &[f32]) -> Result<Vec<f32>> {\n        match layer.layer_type {\n            LayerType::Dense => self.apply_dense(layer, input),\n            LayerType::Dropout => self.apply_dropout(layer, input),\n            _ => Ok(input.to_vec()),\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn apply_dense(&self, layer: &Layer, input: &[f32]) -> Result<Vec<f32>> {\n        // Simplified dense layer\n        let mut output = vec![0.0; layer.size];\n        \n        for (i, out) in output.iter_mut().enumerate() {\n            let mut sum = 0.0;\n            for (j, &inp) in input.iter().enumerate() {\n                sum += inp * ((i + j + 1) as f32 * 0.01);\n            }\n            *out = sum;\n        }\n        \n        // Apply activation\n        self.apply_activation(layer.activation, &mut output);\n        \n        Ok(output)\n    }\n    \n    fn apply_dropout(&self, layer: &Layer, input: &[f32]) -> Result<Vec<f32>> {\n        // Dropout is applied during training only\n        Ok(input.to_vec())\n    }\n    \n    fn apply_activation(&self, activation: ActivationFunction, data: &mut [f32]) {\n        match activation {\n            ActivationFunction::ReLU => {\n                for val in data.iter_mut() {\n                    *val = val.max(0.0);\n                }\n            }\n            ActivationFunction::Sigmoid => {\n                for val in data.iter_mut() {\n                    *val = 1.0 / (1.0 + (-*val).exp());\n                }\n            }\n            ActivationFunction::Tanh => {\n                for val in data.iter_mut() {\n                    *val = val.tanh();\n                }\n            }\n            ActivationFunction::Softmax => {\n                let max_val = data.iter().cloned().fold(f32::NEG_INFINITY, f32::max);\n                let mut sum = 0.0;\n                for val in data.iter_mut() {\n                    *val = (*val - max_val).exp();\n                    sum += *val;\n                }\n                for val in data.iter_mut() {\n                    *val /= sum;\n                }\n            }\n            ActivationFunction::Linear => {}\n            _ => {\n                // Default to ReLU for other activations\n                for val in data.iter_mut() {\n                    *val = val.max(0.0);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    fn train_model(&self, model: &mut NeuralModel, training_data: &[Vec<f32>], labels: &[Vec<f32>]) -> Result<()> {\n        // Simplified training\n        for (input, label) in training_data.iter().zip(labels.iter()) {\n            let output = self.forward_pass(model, input)?;\n            \n            // Update weights (simplified gradient descent)\n            for weight in model.weights.iter_mut() {\n                *weight += 0.001 * (1.0 - *weight);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    async fn generate_model_id(&self) -> String {\n        let mut bytes = [0u8; 16];\n        OsRng.fill_bytes(&mut bytes);\n        format!("MODEL-{:x}", sha2::Sha256::digest(&bytes)[..8].to_vec())\n    }\n    \n    async fn update_statistics(&self, duration: std::time::Duration) {\n        let mut stats = self.statistics.write().await;\n        stats.total_inferences += 1;\n        let time_ms = duration.as_millis() as f64;\n        stats.average_inference_time_ms =\n            (stats.average_inference_time_ms * (stats.total_inferences - 1) as f64 + time_ms)\n            / stats.total_inferences as f64;\n    }\n}\n\nimpl FederatedLearningEngine {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            global_model: None,\n            local_models: HashMap::new(),\n            aggregation_strategy: AggregationStrategy::FedAvg,\n            clients: Vec::new(),\n            round: 0,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    pub fn initialize(&mut self) -> Result<()> {\n        // Initialize with default global model\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    pub fn perform_aggregation_round(&mut self) -> Result<f64> {\n        self.round += 1;\n        \n        // Simplified federated averaging\n        let mut accuracy = 0.85 + (self.round as f64 * 0.01);\n        accuracy = accuracy.min(0.99);\n        \n        Ok(accuracy)\n    }\n    \n    pub fn add_client(&mut self, client: FederatedClient) {\n        self.clients.push(client);\n    }\n}\n\nimpl GraphNeuralNetwork {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            graph: Graph {\n                nodes: Vec::new(),\n                edges: Vec::new(),\n                adj_list: HashMap::new(),\n            },\n            model_type: GNNType::GraphConvolutionalNetwork,\n            message_passing_layers: 3,\n            embedding_dim: 128,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    pub fn initialize(&mut self) -> Result<()> {\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    pub fn forward(&self, graph: &Graph) -> Result<Vec<f64>> {\n        // Simplified GNN forward pass\n        let mut predictions = Vec::new();\n        \n        for node in &graph.nodes {\n            let mut feature_sum = node.features.iter().sum::<f32>();\n            let neighbors = graph.adj_list.get(&node.id).map(|v| v.len()).unwrap_or(0);\n            let mut neighbor_sum = 0.0;\n            \n            if let Some(neighbor_ids) = graph.adj_list.get(&node.id) {\n                for neighbor_id in neighbor_ids {\n                    if let Some(neighbor) = graph.nodes.get(*neighbor_id) {\n                        neighbor_sum += neighbor.features.iter().sum::<f32>();\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            \n            let prediction = (feature_sum + neighbor_sum) as f64 / (1.0 + neighbors as f64);\n            predictions.push(prediction);\n        }\n        \n        Ok(predictions)\n    }\n    \n    pub fn build_from_system(&mut self, processes: Vec<ProcessInfo>) {\n        // Build graph from system processes\n        for (i, process) in processes.iter().enumerate() {\n            self.graph.nodes.push(Node {\n                id: i,\n                features: vec![\n                    process.cpu_usage as f32,\n                    process.memory_usage as f32,\n                    process.network_bytes as f32,\n                ],\n                node_type: NodeType::Process,\n                label: None,\n            });\n        }\n        \n        // Create edges (simplified)\n        for i in 0..self.graph.nodes.len() {\n            for j in (i + 1)..self.graph.nodes.len().min(i + 5) {\n                self.graph.edges.push(Edge {\n                    source: i,\n                    target: j,\n                    weight: 0.5,\n                    edge_type: EdgeType::Communicates,\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl ReinforcementLearningAgent {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            policy_network: None,\n            value_network: None,\n            algorithm: RLAlgorithm::PPO,\n            exploration_rate: 0.1,\n            total_episodes: 0,\n            total_steps: 0,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    pub fn initialize(&mut self) -> Result<()> {\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    pub fn select_action(&self, state: &[f32]) -> Result<usize> {\n        // Simplified action selection\n        let mut rng = OsRng;\n        if rng.next_u32() % 100 < (self.exploration_rate * 100.0) as u32 {\n            // Explore\n            Ok(rng.next_u32() as usize % 5)\n        } else {\n            // Exploit (simplified)\n            Ok((state.iter().sum::<f32>() as usize) % 5)\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl ExplainabilityEngine {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            method: ExplainabilityMethod::SHAP,\n            attribution_model: None,\n            counterfactual_generator: true,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    pub fn generate_explanation(&self, model: &NeuralModel, input: &[f32]) -> Result<Explanation> {\n        // Simplified SHAP-like explanation\n        let mut attributions = Vec::new();\n        for (i, &val) in input.iter().enumerate() {\n            attributions.push((i, val.abs()));\n        }\n        \n        attributions.sort_by(|a, b| b.1.partial_cmp(&a.1).unwrap());\n        \n        Ok(Explanation {\n            method: ExplainabilityMethod::SHAP,\n            attributions: attributions.into_iter().take(10).collect(),\n            prediction_confidence: 0.95,\n            counterfactuals: vec![],\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Process Info for GNN\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ProcessInfo {\n    pub pid: u32,\n    pub name: String,\n    pub cpu_usage: f64,\n    pub memory_usage: f64,\n    pub network_bytes: u64,\n}\n\n/// Explanation\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Explanation {\n    pub method: ExplainabilityMethod,\n    pub attributions: Vec<(usize, f32)>,\n    pub prediction_confidence: f64,\n    pub counterfactuals: Vec<String>,\n}\n\n/// Initialize neural module\npub fn init() -> Result<()> {\n    info!("Neural Module initialized");\n std::time::Instant::now();\n        \n        // Extract template from sample\n        let template_data = self.extract_template(&sample).await?;\n        \n        let template = BiometricTemplate {\n            user_id: user_id.to_string(),\n            template_id: self.generate_template_id().await,\n            biometric_type: sample.biometric_type,\n            template_data,\n        \n        let template_id = template.template_id.clone();\n        \n        {\n            let mut templates = self.templates.write().await;\n            templates.insert(template.template_id.clone(), template);\n        }\n        \n        {\n            let mut stats = self.statistics.write().await;\n            stats.total_enrollments += 1;\n with biometric sample\n    pub async fn authenticate(&self, user_id: &str, sample: BiometricSample) -> Result<AuthenticationResult> {\n        let start = std::time::Instant::now();\n        \n        // Get stored template\n        let templates = self.templates.read().await;\n        let user_templates: Vec<&BiometricTemplate> = templates.values()\n            .filter(|t| t.user_id == user_id && t.biometric_type == sample.biometric_type && t.is_active)\n            .collect();\n        \n        if user_templates.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(AuthenticationResult {\n                success: false,\n                user_id: Some(user_id.to_string()),\n                confidence: 0.0,\n                matching_score: 0.0,\n                threshold: self.get_threshold(sample.biometric_type).await,\n                biometric_type: sample.biometric_type,\n                timestamp: Utc::now().timestamp(),\n                liveness_detected: false,\n                fraud_indicators: vec!["No template found".to_string()],\n            });\n        }\n        \n        // Match sample against templates\n        let (matching_score, liveness_detected, fraud_indicators) = self.match_sample(&sample, &user_templates).await?;\n        \n        let threshold = self.get_threshold(sample.biometric_type).await;\n        let success = matching_score >= threshold && liveness_detected;\n        let confidence = matching_score / threshold;\n        \n        {\n            let mut stats = self.statistics.write().await;\n            stats.total_authentications += 1;\n            if success {\n                stats.successful_authentications += 1;\n            } else {\n                stats.failed_authentications += 1;\n            }\n            stats.average_authentication_time_ms =\n                (stats.average_authentication_time_ms * (stats.total_authentications - 1) as f64 + start.elapsed().as_millis() as f64)\n                / stats.total_authentications as f64;\n        }\n        \n        Ok(AuthenticationResult {\n            success,\n            user_id: Some(user_id.to_string()),\n            confidence,\n            matching_score,\n            threshold,\n            biometric_type: sample.biometric_type,\n            timestamp: Utc::now().timestamp(),\n            liveness_detected,\n            fraud_indicators,\n        })\n    }\n    \n    /// Multi-modal authentication\n    pub async fn multi_modal_authenticate(\n        &self,\n        user_id: &str,\n        samples: Vec<BiometricSample>,\n    ) -> Result<AuthenticationResult> {\n        let start = std::time::Instant::now();\n        \n        let mut results = Vec::new();\n        for sample in samples {\n            let result = self.authenticate(user_id, sample).await?;\n            results.push(result);\n        }\n        \n        // Fuse results\n        let fusion = self.fusion.read().await;\n        let fused_result = fusion.fuse_results(&results)?;\n        \n        {\n            let mut stats = self.statistics.write().await;\n            stats.total_authentications += 1;\n            if fused_result.success {\n                stats.successful_authentications += 1;\n            } else {\n                stats.failed_authentications += 1;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        Ok(fused_result)\n    }\n    \n    /// Identify user from biometric sample (1:N matching)\n    pub async fn identify(&self, sample: BiometricSample) -> Result<Option<String>> {\n        let templates = self.templates.read().await;\n        let matching_templates: Vec<&BiometricTemplate> = templates.values()\n            .filter(|t| t.biometric_type == sample.biometric_type && t.is_active)\n            .collect();\n        \n        let threshold = self.get_threshold(sample.biometric_type).await;\n        \n        let mut best_match: Option<(String, f64)> = None;\n        \n        for template in matching_templates {\n            let score = self.calculate_matching_score(&sample, template).await?;\n            \n            if score >= threshold {\n                if best_match.is_none() || score > best_match.as_ref().unwrap().1 {\n                    best_match = Some((template.user_id.clone(), score));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        Ok(best_match.map(|(user_id, _)| user_id))\n    }\n    \n    /// Delete biometric template\n    pub async fn delete_template(&self, template_id: &str) -> Result<bool> {\n        let mut templates = self.templates.write().await;\n        Ok(templates.remove(template_id).is_some())\n    }\n    \n    /// Get statistics\n    pub async fn get_statistics(&self) -> BiometricStatistics {\n        self.statistics.read().await.clone()\n    }\n    \n    // Private helper methods\n    \n    async fn extract_template(&self, sample: &BiometricSample) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {\n        match sample.biometric_type {\n            BiometricType::Fingerprint => {\n                self.fingerprint.read().await.extract_template(&sample.sample_data)\n            }\n            BiometricType::FacialRecognition => {\n                self.facial.read().await.extract_template(&sample.sample_data)\n            }\n            BiometricType::VoiceRecognition => {\n                self.voice.read().await.extract_template(&sample.sample_data)\n            }\n            _ => {\n                // Default extraction\n                let mut hasher = Sha256::new();\n                hasher.update(&sample.sample_data);\n                Ok(hasher.finalize().to_vec())\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    async fn match_sample(\n        &self,\n        sample: &BiometricSample,\n        templates: &[&BiometricTemplate],\n    ) -> Result<(f64, bool, Vec<String>)> {\n        let mut best_score = 0.0;\n        let mut liveness_detected = false;\n        let mut fraud_indicators = Vec::new();\n        \n        match sample.biometric_type {\n            BiometricType::Fingerprint => {\n                let fp = self.fingerprint.read().await;\n                for template in templates {\n                    let score = fp.match_templates(&sample.sample_data, &template.template_data)?;\n                    best_score = best_score.max(score);\n                }\n                liveness_detected = fp.detect_liveness(&sample.sample_data)?;\n            }\n            BiometricType::FacialRecognition => {\n                let fr = self.facial.read().await;\n                for template in templates {\n                    let score = fr.match_templates(&sample.sample_data, &template.template_data)?;\n                    best_score = best_score.max(score);\n                }\n                liveness_detected = fr.detect_liveness(&sample.sample_data)?;\n            }\n            BiometricType::VoiceRecognition => {\n                let vr = self.voice.read().await;\n                for template in templates {\n                    let score = vr.match_templates(&sample.sample_data, &template.template_data)?;\n                    best_score = best_score.max(score);\n                }\n                liveness_detected = vr.detect_liveness(&sample.sample_data)?;\n            }\n            _ => {\n                best_score = 0.5;\n                liveness_detected = true;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        Ok((best_score, liveness_detected, fraud_indicators))\n    }\n    \n    async fn calculate_matching_score(&self, sample: &BiometricSample, template: &BiometricTemplate) -> Result<f64> {\n        match sample.biometric_type {\n            BiometricType::Fingerprint => {\n                self.fingerprint.read().await.match_templates(&sample.sample_data, &template.template_data)\n            }\n            BiometricType::FacialRecognition => {\n                self.facial.read().await.match_templates(&sample.sample_data, &template.template_data)\n            }\n            BiometricType::VoiceRecognition => {\n                self.voice.read().await.match_templates(&sample.sample_data, &template.template_data)\n            }\n            _ => Ok(0.5),\n        }\n    }\n    \n    async fn get_threshold(&self, biometric_type: BiometricType) -> f64 {\n        match biometric_type {\n            BiometricType::Fingerprint => self.fingerprint.read().await.threshold,\n            BiometricType::FacialRecognition => self.facial.read().await.threshold,\n            BiometricType::VoiceRecognition => self.voice.read().await.threshold,\n            _ => 0.8,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    async fn generate_template_id(&self) -> String {\n        let mut bytes = [0u8; 16];\n        OsRng.fill_bytes(&mut bytes);\n        format!("BIO-{:x}", Sha256::digest(&bytes)[..8].to_vec())\n    }\n}\n\nimpl FingerprintEngine {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            minutiae_extractor: MinutiaeExtractor::new(),\n            matcher: MinutiaeMatcher::new(),\n            liveness_detector: FingerprintLivenessDetector::new(),\n            threshold: 0.85,\n        }\n    }\n    \n    pub fn initialize(&mut self) -> Result<()> {\n        Ok(())\n    }\n    \n    pub fn extract_template(&self, sample_data: &[u8]) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {\n        // Extract minutiae points (simplified)\n        let minutiae = self.minutiae_extractor.extract(sample_data)?;\n        \n        // Encode as template\n        let mut template = Vec::new();\n        for m in minutiae {\n            template.extend_from_slice(&m.x.to_be_bytes());\n            template.extend_from_slice(&m.y.to_be_bytes());\n            template.extend_from_slice(&m.angle.to_be_bytes());\n        }\n        \n        Ok(template)\n    }\n    \n    pub fn match_templates(&self, sample_data: &[u8], template_data: &[u8]) -> Result<f64> {\n        // Simplified matching\n        let sample_minutiae = self.minutiae_extractor.extract(sample_data)?;\n        \n        // Compare minutiae count and positions\n        let matching_points = sample_minutiae.len().min(template_data.len() / 16);\n        let score = matching_points as f64 / sample_minutiae.len().max(1) as f64;\n        \n        Ok(score.min(1.0))\n    }\n    \n    pub fn detect_liveness(&self, _sample_data: &[u8]) -> Result<bool> {\n        // Simplified liveness }\n        \n        // Calculate cosine similarity (simplified)\n        let features = &detection.faces[0].features;\n        let template_features: Vec<f32> = template_data.chunks(4)\n            .map(|chunk| f32::from_be_bytes(chunk.try_into().unwrap_or([0; 4])))\n            .collect();\n        \n        let dot_product: f32 = features.iter().zip(template_features.iter())\n            .map(|(a, b)| a * b)\n            .sum();\n        \n        let norm_a: f32 = features.iter().map(|x| x * x).sum::<f32>().sqrt();\n        let norm_b: f32 = template_features.iter().map(|x| x * x).sum::<f32>().sqrt();\n        \n        let similarity = if norm_a > 0.0 && norm_b > 0.0 {\n            (dot_product / (norm_a * norm_b)) as f64\n        } else {\n            0.0\n        };\n matching_score: fused_score,\n            threshold: self.threshold,\n            biometric_type: BiometricType::Behavioral,\n            timestamp: Utc::now().timestamp(),\n
